What I like about Spiritbox is that they're just absolutely excellent at what they're doing.   The music isn't reinventing anything and isn't really outside the box - they're blending current, digestible, relevant mainstream pop and metal musical trends that I happen to enjoy with a good degree of complexity, and executing it perfectly. Courtney has a smooth, beautiful voice and perfect technique in all the styles she sings in, and the musical construction is grade-A every time.  On top of that, every now and then they'll throw in something really unique and stick to their roots & original sound that makes it stand out - whether it's an odd, unique melody or bridge, or some unfamiliar haunting synth or a touch of avant- garde vocals, so that it never gets too stale, and the lyrics are always written in a way that can be interpreted different and relatable at least in parts by a wide audience.

I used to be a musician, I had a few close calls with success. Life got the best of me and I hung up what was left of my guitars and sold everything else and in late December 2019 and walked away. I wasn't even interested in music anymore. Spiritbox was the band that brought a little spark back to my musical life. I don't think I'll ever be in a band again, but I may poke around in my own studio just to see if I can make it fun again and to mute the other things that are going on in my life for a while and it is hugely because of this band. I have a small list of bands that have affected me this much. KISS, Gravity Kills, KMFDM, CombiChrist, Prince, Celldweller, and now Spiritbox.
